Filters based on Envoy response flags (errors, timeouts, etc.)\\n8. **GrpcStatusFilter** - Filters based on gRPC status codes (with HTTP status fallback)\\n9. **LogTypeFilter** - Filters based on access log type (HTTP, TCP, etc.)\\n10. **MetadataFilter** - Filters based on dynamic metadata presence or values\\n11. **AndFilter** - Logical AND composition of sub-filters\\n12. **OrFilter** - Logical OR composition of sub-filters\\n\\n### Extension Filters\\n\\n13. **CEL Filter** (in `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/`)\\n   - Evaluates Common Expression Language (CEL) expressions\\n   - Location: `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/cel.h` (CELAccessLogExtensionFilter)\\n   - Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/v3/cel.proto`\\n   -
